  patient_name VARCHAR(50),
  age INT,
  gender VARCHAR(10)
);


CREATE TABLE appointment (
  appointment_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  patient_id INT,
  doctor_id INT,
  appointment_date DATE,
  appointment_time TIME
);
</t><stat>select doctor.doctor_name, patient.age from doctor join appointment on doctor.doctor_id = appointment.doctor_id join patient on patient.patient_id = appointment.patient_id;</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE medical_record (

  prescription VARCHAR(100)

  prescription VARCHAR(100)
);
